7. GLOBAL SUMMARY — RULE THRESHOLDS
   Hybrid approach:
     - Global absolute thresholds (mean+kσ from training) for ratios & packet sizes
     - Per-IP fixed 3x multiplier for volume metrics (flows, bytes, destinations)
     - Categorical baseline for anomalous destinations
============================================================

--- Rule: Internal BotNet ---
  Approach: Per-IP deviation with fixed 3x multiplier
  Signal: test_flows > 3x train_flows AND > 500
  Signal: test_dsts   > 3x train_dsts   AND > 20
  Training flow count reference:
    194 IPs, min=193.00, p5=1196.45, median=4616.50, mean=4699.45, std=2172.59, p95=8502.35, p99=9690.62, max=11082.00
    >> threshold = 95th percentile = 8502.35
  Training unique dst IPs reference:
    194 IPs, min=23.00, p5=56.00, median=124.50, mean=126.10, std=42.59, p95=202.35, p99=226.21, max=236.00
    >> threshold = 95th percentile = 202.35

--- Rule: Data Exfiltration via DNS ---
  Approach: Global threshold for DNS/HTTPS ratio + per-IP 3x for DNS volume
  Global threshold: dns_https_flow_ratio > 0.2 (above training max of 0.19)
  Per-IP: test_dns_flows > 3x train_dns_flows AND > 100
  Per-IP: test_dns_up > 3x train_dns_up AND > 10,000
  Training DNS/HTTPS ratio reference:
    194 IPs, min=0.09, p5=0.12, median=0.14, mean=0.14, std=0.01, p95=0.16, p99=0.17, max=0.19
    >> threshold = mean + 2σ = 0.16

--- Rule: Data Exfiltration via HTTPS ---
  Approach: Global threshold for up/down ratio + per-IP 3x for HTTPS volume
  Global threshold: https_up_down_ratio > 0.12 (training mean + 3σ, mean≈0.11, σ≈0.003)
  Per-IP: test_https_up > 3x train_https_up AND > 100,000
  Ratio signal requires AND with volume surge

--- Rule: C&C via DNS ---
  Approach: Global threshold for DNS packet size + per-IP 3x for DNS flows
  Global threshold: dns_mean_up > 217 bytes (training mean + 5σ, mean≈199.9, σ≈3.47)
  Per-IP: test_dns_flows > 3x train_dns_flows AND > 100
  Training DNS mean upload reference:
    194 IPs, min=189.57, p5=194.17, median=199.89, mean=199.89, std=3.47, p95=205.37, p99=209.24, max=212.58
    >> threshold = mean + 3σ = 210.31

--- Rule: Anomalous External Destinations ---
  Approach: Global categorical baseline
  Baseline: countries seen by any IP in training.
  Rule: flag IP if test data contacts a country NOT in training, with >= 3 flows.
  194 IPs have country data from training.
  Global country set seen in training (36): ['AE', 'AT', 'AU', 'BE', 'BH', 'BR', 'CA', 'CH', 'CL', 'CN', 'DE', 'ES', 'FR', 'GB', 'HK', 'ID', 'IE', 'IL', 'IN', 'IT', 'JP', 'KR', 'MX', 'MY', 'NL', 'NO', 'PH', 'PT', 'RO', 'SA', 'SE', 'SG', 'TH', 'TW', 'US', 'ZA']

--- Rule: External User Behavior ---
  Approach: Per-IP temporal (off-hours vs training max) + global CV floor
  Global CV floor (minimum across all training IPs): 3.54
  Rule: flag external IP if test_CV < 3.54 (more regular than any training IP)
        OR off-hours > 50% of test flows outside training active hours
        OR both (AND logic)
Done.
